< review>
The course is always in very good condition, which based on the rates it should be. The driving range offers either mats (with overhead cover) or grass for your choosing. < Review>
Decent driving range, has 3 sections: Covered artificial turf tees, grass lesson area, and grass area for irons only. Problem is if you actually want to practice your drives you have to be at the covered artificial truf tees, and furthermore you need to have your own rubber tees for them as you are not allowed to practice drives in front of them.

If you try to tee up in front of them you will get talked to in a very condescending way by an employee even if you are very nice about it when they ask you to move bacm. Quite frankly it put a damper on my whole experience today as I don't have rubber tees and there's not really a way to set up wood tees on the turf pads so I was unable to practice my drives.

Also the last time I came here was the first time I had been here in years so I went to the pro shop to ask how things worked around here and the employee looked at me like I wasn't very bright and was rather condescending during our interaction. Maybe its because im 21 and they arent fond of people my age, but I don't know. I say this because they seemed cheery with others that were older. However I will say other employees were cheery when they came around to pick up range baskets and I brought my baskets over to them the previous time I was here.

Besides the employee interactions I've had and limitations on being able to practice your drive, its a good range with an automated ball vending machine where you can pay with credit card and get 4 different amounts of balls to choose from at reasonable prices. If you can do it, it's easy to hit for multiple hours at a time. You do want to come early though as the range and parking lot fill up quick.

Also I wish there were more target like things to hit at. It can make practicing different distances kind of boring as its mostly just flags at longer distances.<//Review>

< review>
Great 9 hole spot to work on your short game.  Hole 5 is a lot like the 17th at Bartley Cavanaugh in south Sacramento . . . a par 3 on a little peninsula that requires a fairly accurate strike with your pitching wedge to avoid water all around it.  Great for walking.  Very busy on weekend mornings with clubs, tournaments and First Tee.  Best bet is afternoons and weekdays.< /review>

< Review>
My wife and I came here for lunch because of a Groupon offer.  We gave them the coupon before the meal and they accepted it.  But when we got our bill, we found out they didn't apply the coupon.  We asked them about it and the waiter said the coupon's for dinner only.  We asked him to reconsider, he talked to the manager and we ended up being able to use half of the coupon towards the bill and save the other half for dinner the next time we go, which I don't think we will.  I wasn't happy about how they handled the Groupon deal, they should've told us before hand that it's only good for dinner.  And they should've applied the entire coupon towards our meal.

The food itself was not too bad.  The bread and dipping sauce they serve with it is really good.  I got a salmon risotto and I didn't like it.  It was too bland for me.  My wife got the spinach ravioli and she really liked it.</Review>

I basically accidentally walked into there last night. I had intended to go to some junk fastfood place nearby, but somehow, this ristorante attracted me, so I sat down and had dinner there.
I had bruschetta (con pomodoro e basilico) for starters and penne spalti. Both tasted fantastic. The food was authentic italian, not the usual american italian variant, which means it was a lot more to my taste.

<Date>1469159787253</Date><Response>None< /Response><Text>Today I went to Northstate Recycling to redeem both aluminum cans and #1 plastic bottles as a fund raiser for a non-profit organization to which I belong.  We had collected a number of both.....in fact over 140 lbs of cans and about the same of bottles.  The attendant checked us out and gave me the receipt to take into the office to be paid.  Our total pay-out was just over $88.  Knowing that aluminum cans are currently over $1.60 per pound I questioned the clerk as to why we received so little.  I was then (after the fact) informed that since we had more than 100 pounds of cans we were paid scrap metal prices....... 20 cents per pound!  According to the clerk this is required by state legislation.  That does sound like something our state legislators would do, but I am quite sure that the attendant who checked us out was aware of that fact.  I would think that in an honest business the attendant would inform the customer of this fact and give them the opportunity to turn in less than 100 pounds.  Our total on just 100 pounds of aluminum cans would have been $160.00, as opposed to the $29 we actually received for the whole 145 pounds.  I would have been better off to have given 40 pounds of cans to the person in line behind me......I'd have walked away with more money for our organization.  In fact, my husband was with me and all the attendant would have had to do is to inform us of the rule and we could have divided our cans in half and each received payments.  I am amazed that a business that has been in Redding for such a long time is so obviously dishonest in their dealings with the public.  I don't know if the policy is displayed for the public to see, but if it is I can say it is not prominently displayed.  Beware of the business practices of this company.  If they can cheat you, they will.</Text>< GmapID>

< Name>
Rama Duvvuri<//Name>
<Date>1530047162956<//Date><rate>2<//rate>< Text>
UPDATED review:  lowered to 2 stars.

I've been here a few times now, 3 times eat in and once take out.  The take out was the only positive experience I've had.

The pros - they did a good job in remodeling this space, and it has potential to be good.  The pizza itself (veggiemore in particular) is quite good and probably worth their premium price.

The downside -this restaurant seems very poorly managed.  The lunch buffet appears a good deal, but they've stopped including drinks.  They also make you re-use your plates if you go back up to the buffet - I'm pretty sure this is a health code violation.

They also don't have very much pizza on the buffet.  Today when I went in, they had half a pizza left for my party of three, and I pointed that out to them, and they said they make more as the pizza runs out.  We were there for 30 minutes and they never restocked the pizza.  So we basically paid $30 for half a medium pizza - not a very good value.

Finally, the cleanliness of this place leaves much to be desired - they don't seem to bus their tables often, nor do they wipe the tables well.

If you do give them a chance, I'd suggest carry out - the in restaurant experience is very disappointing for a place that had potential.</Text>
